[[1]]$value
function (Xtrain.rds, y.rds, Xtest.rds, data_checks_func, train_func, 
    iter, pct_train) 
{
    Xtrain <- readRDS(Xtrain.rds)
    Xtest <- readRDS(Xtest.rds)
    y <- readRDS(y.rds)
    data_checks_func(Xtrain, Xtest, y)
    OUTPUT <- train_func(Xtrain, Xtest, y, iter, pct_train)
}

[[2]]
[[2]]$value
function (M, model_dir, meta) 
{
    require(Rtsne)
    require(doMC)
    require(data.table)
    if (!dir.exists(model_dir)) {
        dir.create(model_dir)
    }
    registerDoMC(2)
    grid = expand.grid(PCA = c(T), perplexity = c(20, 50, 100, 
        250), scale_it = c(T), asinh_it = c(T, F))
    A <- foreach(i = 1:nrow(grid), .verbose = T) %dopar% {
        PCA <- grid[i, "PCA"]
        perplexity <- grid[i, "perplexity"]
        scale_it <- grid[i, "scale_it"]
        asinh_it <- grid[i, "asinh_it"]
        data <- copy(M)
        if (asinh_it) 
            data <- asinh(data)
        if (scale_it) 
            data <- scale(data)
        print(i)
        z <- Rtsne(X = data[1:300, ], perplexity = perplexity, 
            pca = PCA, theta = 0.75, verbose = T, max_iter = 1000, 
            dims = 2, initial_dims = 50)
        z
    }
    saveRDS(A, file.path(model_dir, "TSNE_list.rds"))
}

[[3]]
[[3]]$value
function (seed, missing = NULL) 
{
    set.seed(seed)
    params = list(booster = "gblinear", objective = "binary:logistic", 
        eval_metric = "logloss", eta = runif(1, 0.01, 0.2), subsample = runif(1, 
            0.4, 0.6), nrounds = 1000, lambda = runif(1, 0.25, 
            1.5), alpha = 0, lambda_bias = runif(1, 0, 0.1), 
        base_score = runif(1, 0.5, 0.8), nthread = 12, missing = missing)
    return(params)
}

[[4]]
[[4]]$value
function (seed, missing = NULL) 
{
    set.seed(seed)
    params = list(booster = "gbtree", objective = "binary:logistic", 
        eval_metric = "logloss", max.depth = sample(3:12, 1), 
        eta = runif(1, 0.01, 0.2), gamma = runif(1, 0, 2.5), 
        min_child_weight = runif(1, 0, 5), subsample = runif(1, 
            0.4, 0.6), colsample_bytree = runif(1, 0.3, 0.9), 
        nrounds = 1000, lambda = runif(1, 0.25, 1.5), alpha = 0, 
        base_score = runif(1, 0.5, 0.8), nthread = 12, missing = missing)
    return(params)
}

[[5]]
[[5]]$value
function (Xtrain, Xtest, y, iter, pct_train) 
{
    OUTPUT <- init_OUPUT(nrow(Xtrain), nrow(Xtest), iter, pct_train)
    missing <- attr(Xtrain, "missing")
    dtest <- xgb.DMatrix(Xtest, missing = missing)
    for (i in 1:iter) {
        cat("building model", i, "\n\n")
        idx <- OUTPUT$IDX[, i]
        dtrain <- xgb.DMatrix(Xtrain[idx, ], missing = missing, 
            label = y[idx])
        dvalid <- xgb.DMatrix(Xtrain[-idx, ], missing = missing, 
            label = y[-idx])
        param = list(booster = "gbtree", objective = "binary:logistic", 
            eval_metric = "logloss", max.depth = sample(3:12, 
                1), eta = runif(1, 0.01, 0.2), gamma = runif(1, 
                0, 1), min_child_weight = runif(1, 0, 3), subsample = runif(1, 
                0.4, 0.6), colsample_bytree = runif(1, 0.3, 0.9), 
            nrounds = 1000, lambda = runif(1, 0.25, 1.5), alpha = 0, 
            base_score = mean(y) + runif(1, -0.1, 0.1), nthread = 12)
        model <- xgb.train(early.stop.round = 20, watchlist = list(valid_err = dvalid), 
            print.every.n = 50, param = param, data = dtrain, 
            nrounds = param$nrounds, maximize = F, verbose = 1)
        OUTPUT$PCV[-idx, i] <- predict(model, newdata = dvalid, 
            ntreelimit = model$bestInd)
        OUTPUT$PT[, i] <- predict(model, newdata = dtest, ntreelimit = model$bestInd)
        OUTPUT$DATA[[i]] <- list(param = param, rounds = model$bestInd, 
            cv_score = model$bestScore)
    }
    return(OUTPUT)
}

[[5]]$visible

[[6]]
[[6]]$value
function (Xtrain, Xtest, y) 
{
    stopifnot(unique(y) %in% c(0, 1))
    stopifnot(length(y) == nrow(Xtrain))
    stopifnot(ncol(Xtrain) == ncol(Xtest))
    stopifnot(colnames(Xtrain) == colnames(Xtest))
    cat("PASS! - yo  data is pretty clean...")
}

[[6]]$visible
[1] FALSE


[[7]]
[[7]]$value
function (n_train_full, n_test_full, iter, pct_train) 
{
    n_train_samp <- round(pct_train * n_train_full)
    return(list(PCV = matrix(NA_real_, nrow = n_train_full, ncol = iter), 
        PT = matrix(NA_real_, nrow = n_test_full, ncol = iter), 
        IDX = sapply(1:iter, function(z) sample(n_train_full, 
            n_train_samp)), DATA = vector(mode = "list", length = iter)))
}

[[8]]
[[8]]$value
function (DT, val = -999) 
{
    Z <- copy(DT)
    for (col in seq_along(Z)) set(Z, i = which(is.na(Z[[col]])), 
        j = col, value = -999)
    return(Z)
}

[[9]]
[[9]]$value
function (X, fac_cols, max_cat = 1024) 
{
    X_fac <- copy(X[, fac_cols, with = F])
    X_fac[, `:=`((fac_cols), lapply(.SD, factor, exclude = NULL)), 
        .SDcols = fac_cols]
    fac_count_cols = paste("counts", fac_cols, sep = "_")
    X_fac[, `:=`((fac_count_cols), lapply(.SD, function(col) table(col)[col])), 
        .SDcols = fac_cols]
    levs <- X_fac[, lapply(.SD, function(i) length(levels(i))), 
        .SDcols = fac_cols]
    fix_cols <- names(levs)[which(levs >= max_cat)]
    for (f in fix_cols) {
        lev <- levels(X_fac[, get(f)])
        low_n <- length(lev) - max_cat
        low <- names(sort(table(X_fac[, get(f)]))[1:low_n])
        X_fac[get(f) %in% low, `:=`((f), "low")]
        X_fac[, `:=`((f), factor(get(f)))]
    }
    M <- sparse.model.matrix(~. - 1, data = X_fac)
    return(M)
}
